0been%20suggested%20that%20the%20term%20originated%20earlier%20than%20this,%20in%20Yorkshire.%20%20Among%20noted%20players%20who%20have%20bowled%20the%20chinaman%20is%20Denis%20Compton,%20who%20specialised%20in%20the%20delivery%20when%20bowling.%20%20Although%20better%20known%20for%20fast%20bowling%20and%20orthodox%20slow%20left%20arm,%20Garfield%20Sobers%20could%20also%20use%20the%20chinaman%20to%20good%20effect.%20%20In%20cricket's%20modern%20era,%20Brad%20Hogg%20is%20a%20natural%20spinner%20of%20the%20ball%20who%20popularized%20the%20chinaman%20delivery%20and%20has%20one%20of%20the%20most%20well-disguised%20wrong-un's.%20%20He%20was%20a%20member%20of%20Australia's%20victorious%202003%20and%202007%20Cricket%20World%20Cup%20teams,%20picking%20up%2013%20wickets%20in%202003%20and%2021%20wickets%20in%202007.%20%20Kuldeep%20Yadav%20is%20a%20Chinaman%20bowler%20from%20India%20who%20made%20a%20successful%20debut%20in%20the%204th%20test%20against%20Australia%20in%20Dharamsala%20on%2025%20March%202017%20by%20picking%20up%204%20wickets%20in%20the%20first%20innings.%20%20He%20is%20the%20first%20Indian%20left%20arm%20chinaman%20bowler%20to%20debut%20in%20tests.%20%20Paul%20Adams%20has%20been%20a%20noted%20chinaman%20bowler%20from%20South%20Africa%20who%20played%2045%20test%20matches%20between%201995-2004. Left-arm%20unorthodox%20spin,%20also%20known%20as%20slow%20left%20arm%20chinaman,%20is%20a%20type%20of%20left%20arm%20wrist%20off%20spin%20bowling%20in%20the%20sport%20of%20cricket.%20%20Left-arm%20unorthodox%20spin%20bowlers%20use%20wrist%20spin%20to%20spin%20the%20ball,%20and%20make%20it%20deviate,%20or%20"turn"%20from%20left%20to%20right%20after%20pitching.%20%20The%20direction%20of%20turn%20is%20the%20same%20as%20that%20of%20a%20traditional%20right-handed%20off%20spin%20bowler;%20however,%20the%20ball%20will%20usually%20turn%20more%20sharply%20due%20to%20the%20spin%20being%20imparted%20predominantly%20by%20the%20wrist.%20%20Some%20left-arm%20unorthodox%20bowlers%20also%20bowl%20the%20equivalent%20of%20a%20"googly",%20(or%20"wrong'un"),%20which%20turns%20from%20right%20to%20left%20on%20the%20pitch.%20%20The%20ball%20turns%20away%20from%20the%20right-handed%20batsman,%20as%20if%20the%20bowler%20were%20an%20orthodox%20left-arm%20spinner.%20%20In%20cricketing%20parlance,%20the%20word%20"chinaman"%20is%20used%20to%20describe%20the%20stock%20delivery%20of%20a%20left-arm%20"unorthodox"%20spin%20bowler%20(though%20some%20reserve%20it%20for%20the%20googly%20delivery%20).%20%20The%20origin%20of%20the%20term%20is%20uncertain.%20%20One%20version%20relates%20to%20a%20Test%20match%20played%20between%20England%20and%20the%20West%20Indies%20at%20Old%20Trafford%20in%201933.%20%20Ellis%20"Puss"%20Achong,%20a%20player%20of%20Chinese%20origin,%20was%20a%20left-arm%20orthodox%20spinner,%20playing%20for%20the%20West%20Indies.%20%20He%20had%20Walter%20Robins%20stumped%20off%20a%20surprise%20delivery%20that%20spun%20into%20the%20right-hander%20from%20outside%20the%20off%20stump.%20%20As%20he%20walked%20back%20to%20the%20pavilion,%20Robins%20reportedly%20said%20to%20the%20umpire,%20"fancy%20being%20done%20by%20a%20bloody%20Chinaman!",%20leading%20to%20the%20popularity%20of%20the%20term%20in%20England,%20and%20subsequently,%20in%20the%20rest%20of%20the%20world.%20%20However,%20it%20has%20been%20suggested%20that%20the%20term%20originated%20earlier%20than%20this,%20in%20Yorkshire.%20%20Among%20noted%20players%20who%20have%20bowled%20the%20chinaman%20is%20Denis%20Compton,%20who%20specialised%20in%20the%20delivery%20when%20bowling.%20%20Although%20better%20known%20for%20fast%20bowling%20and%20orthodox%20slow%20left%20arm,%20Garfield%20Sobers%20could%20also%20use%20the%20chinaman%20to%20good%20effect.%20%20In%20cricket's%20modern%20era,%20Brad%20Hogg%20is%20a%20natural%20spinner%20of%20the%20ball%20who%20popularized%20the%20chinaman%20delivery%20and%20has%20one%20of%20the%20most%20well-disguised%20wrong-un's.%20%20He%20was%20a%20member%20of%20Australia's%20victorious%202003%20and%202007%20Cricket%20World%20Cup%20teams,%20picking%20up%2013%20wickets%20in%202003%20and%2021%20wickets%20in%202007.%20%20Kuldeep%20Yadav%20is%20a%20Chinaman%20bowler%20from%20India%20who%20made%20a%20successful%20debut%20in%20the%204th%20test%20against%20Australia%20in%20Dharamsala%20on%2025%20March%202017%20by%20picking%20up%204%20wickets%20in%20the%20first%20innings.%20%20He%20is%20the%20first%20Indian%20left%20arm%20chinaman%20bowler%20to%20debut%20in%20tests.%20%20Paul%20Adams%20has%20been%20a%20noted%20chinaman%20bowler%20from%20South%20Africa%20who%20played%2045%20test%20matches%20between%201995-2004. eak%20and%20the%20topspinner,%20which%20does%20not%20turn%20but%20dips%20sharply%20and%20bounces%20higher%20than%20other%20deliveries.%20%20A%20few%20leg%20spinners%20such%20as%20Abdul%20Qadir,%20Anil%20Kumble,%20Shane%20Warne%20and%20Mushtaq%20Ahmed%20have%20also%20mastered%20the%20flipper,%20a%20delivery%20that%20like%20a%20topspinner%20goes%20straight%20on%20landing,%20but%20floats%20through%20the%20air%20before%20skidding%20and%20keeping%20low,%20often%20dismissing%20batsmen%20leg%20before%20wicket%20or%20bowled.%20%20Another%20variation%20in%20the%20arsenal%20of%20some%20leg%20spinners%20is%20the%20slider,%20a%20leg%20break%20pushed%20out%20of%20the%20hand%20somewhat%20faster,%20so%20that%20it%20does%20not%20spin%20as%20much,%20but%20travels%20more%20straight%20on.%20%20To%20grip%20the%20ball%20for%20a%20leg-spinning%20delivery,%20the%20ball%20is%20placed%20into%20the%20palm%20with%20the%20seam%20parallel%20to%20the%20palm.%20%20The%20first%20two%20fingers%20then%20spread%20and%20grip%20the%20ball,%20and%20the%20third%20and%20fourth%20fingers%20close%20together%20and%20rest%20against%20the%20side%20of%20the%20ball.%20%20The%20first%20bend%20of%20the%20third%20finger%20should%20grasp%20the%20seam.%20%20The%20thumb%20resting%20against%20the%20side%20is%20up%20to%20the%20bowler,%20but%20should%20impart%20no%20pressure.%20%20When%20the%20ball%20is%20bowled,%20the%20third%20finger%20will%20apply%20most%20of%20the%20spin.%20%20The%20wrist%20is%20cocked%20as%20it%20comes%20down%20by%20the%20hip,%20and%20the%20wrist%20moves%20sharply%20from%20right%20to%20left%20as%20the%20ball%20is%20released,%20adding%20more%20spin.%20%20The%20ball%20is%20tossed%20up%20to%20provide%20flight.%20%20The%20batsman%20will%20see%20the%20hand%20with%20the%20palm%20facing%20towards%20them%20when%20the%20ball%20is%20released. eak%20and%20the%20topspinner,%20which%20does%20not%20turn%20but%20dips%20sharply%20and%20bounces%20higher%20than%20other%20deliveries.%20%20A%20few%20leg%20spinners%20such%20as%20Abdul%20Qadir,%20Anil%20Kumble,%20Shane%20Warne%20and%20Mushtaq%20Ahmed%20have%20also%20mastered%20the%20flipper,%20a%20delivery%20that%20like%20a%20topspinner%20goes%20straight%20on%20landing,%20but%20floats%20through%20the%20air%20before%20skidding%20and%20keeping%20low,%20often%20dismissing%20batsmen%20leg%20before%20wicket%20or%20bowled.%20%20Another%20variation%20in%20the%20arsenal%20of%20some%20leg%20spinners%20is%20the%20slider,%20a%20leg%20break%20pushed%20out%20of%20the%20hand%20somewhat%20faster,%20so%20that%20it%20does%20not%20spin%20as%20much,%20but%20travels%20more%20straight%20on.%20%20To%20grip%20the%20ball%20for%20a%20leg-spinning%20delivery,%20the%20ball%20is%20placed%20into%20the%20palm%20with%20the%20seam%20parallel%20to%20the%20palm.%20%20The%20first%20two%20fingers%20then%20spread%20and%20grip%20the%20ball,%20and%20the%20third%20and%20fourth%20fingers%20close%20together%20and%20rest%20against%20the%20side%20of%20the%20ball.%20%20The%20first%20bend%20of%20the%20third%20finger%20should%20grasp%20the%20seam.%20%20The%20thumb%20resting%20against%20the%20side%20is%20up%20to%20the%20bowler,%20but%20should%20impart%20no%20pressure.%20%20When%20the%20ball%20is%20bowled,%20the%20third%20finger%20will%20apply%20most%20of%20the%20spin.%20%20The%20wrist%20is%20cocked%20as%20it%20comes%20down%20by%20the%20hip,%20and%20the%20wrist%20moves%20sharply%20from%20right%20to%20left%20as%20the%20ball%20is%20released,%20adding%20more%20spin.%20%20The%20ball%20is%20tossed%20up%20to%20provide%20flight.%20%20The%20batsman%20will%20see%20the%20hand%20with%20the%20palm%20facing%20towards%20them%20when%20the%20ball%20is%20released. Charles%20Hardin%20Holley%20(September%207,%201936%20�%20February%203,%201959),%20known%20as%20Buddy%20Holly,%20was%20an%20American%20musician%20and%20singer-songwriter%20who%20was%20a%20central%20figure%20of%20mid-1950s%20rock%20and%20roll.%20%20He%20was%20born%20in%20Lubbock,%20Texas,%20to%20a%20musical%20family%20during%20the%20Great%20Depression,%20and%20learned%20to%20play%20guitar%20and%20sing%20alongside%20his%20siblings.%20%20His%20style%20was%20influenced%20by%20gospel%20music,%20country%20music,%20and%20rhythm%20and%20blues%20acts,%20and%20he%20performed%20in%20Lubbock%20with%20his%20friends%20from%20high%20school.%20%20He%20made%20his%20first%20appearance%20on%20local%20television%20in%201952,%20and%20the%20following%20year%20he%20formed%20the%20group%20"Buddy%20and%20Bob"%20with%20his%20friend%20Bob%20Montgomery.%20%20In%201955,%20after%20opening%20for%20Elvis%20Presley,%20he%20decided%20to%20pursue%20a%20career%20in%20music.%20%20He%20opened%20for%20Presley%20three%20times%20that%20year;%20his%20band's%20style%20shifted%20from%20country%20and%20western%20to%20entirely%20rock%20and%20roll.%20%20In%20October%20that%20year,%20when%20he%20opened%20for%20Bill%20Haley%20&%20His%20Comets,%20he%20was%20spotted%20by%20Nashville%20scout%20Eddie%20Crandall,%20who%20helped%20him%20get%20a%20contract%20with%20Decca%20Records.%20%20Holly's%20recording%20sessions%20at%20Decca%20were%20produced%20by%20Owen%20Bradley.%20%20Unhappy%20with%20Bradley's%20control%20in%20the%20studio%20and%20with%20the%20sound%20he%20achieved%20there,%20he%20went%20to%20producer%20Norman%20Petty%20in%20Clovis,%20New%20Mexico,%20and%20recorded%20a%20demo%20of%20"That'll%20Be%20the%20Day",%20among%20other%20songs.%20%20Petty%20became%20the%20band's%20manager%20and%20sent%20the%20demo%20to%20Brunswick%20Records,%20which%20released%20it%20as%20a%20single%20credited%20to%20"The%20Crickets",%20which%20became%20the%20name%20of%20Holly's%20band.%20%20In%20September%201957,%20as%20the%20band%20toured,%20"That'll%20Be%20the%20Day"%20topped%20the%20US%20"Best%20Sellers%20in%20Stores"%20chart%20and%20the%20UK%20Singles%20Chart.%20%20Its%20success%20was%20followed%20in%20October%20by%20another%20major%20hit,%20"Peggy%20Sue".%20%20The%20album%20Chirping%20Crickets,%20released%20in%20November%201957,%20reached%20number%20five%20on%20the%20UK%20Albums%20Chart.%20%20Holly%20made%20his%20second%20appearance%20on%20The%20Ed%20Sullivan%20Show%20in%20January%201958%20and%20soon%20after,%20toured%20Australia%20and%20then%20the%20UK.%20%20In%20early%201959,%20he%20assembled%20a%20new%20band,%20consisting%20of%20future%20country%20music%20star%20Waylon%20Jennings%20(bass),%20famed%20session%20musician%20Tommy%20Allsup%20(guitar),%20and%20Carl%20Bunch%20(drums),%20and%20embarked%20on%20a%20tour%20of%20the%20midwestern%20U.S.%20%20After%20a%20show%20in%20Clear%20Lake,%20Iowa,%20he%20chartered%20an%20airplane%20to%20travel%20to%20his%20next%20show,%20in%20Moorhead,%20Minnesota.%20%20Soon%20after%20takeoff,%20the%20plane%20crashed,%20killing%20him,%20Ritchie%20Valens,%20The%20Big%20Bopper,%20and%20pilot%20Roger%20Peterson%20in%20a%20tragedy%20later%20referred%20to%20by%20Don%20McLean%20as%20"The%20Day%20the%20Music%20Died".%20%20During%20his%20short%20career,%20Holly%20wrote,%20recorded,%20and%20produced%20his%20own%20material.%20%20He%20is%20often%20regarded%20as%20the%20artist%20who%20defined%20the%20traditional%20rock-and-roll%20lineup%20of%20two%20guitars,%20bass,%20and%20drums.%20%20He%20was%20a%20major%20influence%20on%20later%20popular%20music%20artists,%20including%20Bob%20Dylan,%20The%20Beatles,%20The%20Rolling%20Stones,%20Eric%20Clapton,%20and%20Elton%20John.%20%20He%20was%20among%20the%20first%20artists%20inducted%20into%20the%20Rock%20and%20Roll%20Hall%20of%20Fame,%20in%201986.%20%20Rolling%20Stone%20magazine%20ranked%20him%20number%2013%20in%20its%20list%20of%20"100%20Greatest%20Artists". Charles%20Hardin%20Holley%20(September%207,%201936%20�%20February%203,%201959),%20known%20as%20Buddy%20Holly,%20was%20an%20American%20musician%20and%20singer-songwriter%20who%20was%20a%20central%20figure%20of%20mid-1950s%20rock%20and%20roll.%20%20He%20was%20born%20in%20Lubbock,%20Texas,%20to%20a%20musical%20family%20during%20the%20Great%20Depression,%20and%20learned%20to%20play%20guitar%20and%20sing%20alongside%20his%20siblings.%20%20His%20style%20was%20influenced%20by%20gospel%20music,%20country%20music,%20and%20rhythm%20and%20blues%20acts,%20and%20he%20performed%20in%20Lubbock%20with%20his%20friends%20from%20high%20school.%20%20He%20made%20his%20first%20appearance%20on%20local%20television%20in%201952,%20and%20the%20following%20year%20he%20formed%20the%20group%20"Buddy%20and%20Bob"%20with%20his%20friend%20Bob%20Montgomery.%20%20In%201955,%20after%20opening%20for%20Elvis%20Presley,%20he%20decided%20to%20pursue%20a%20career%20in%20music.%20%20He%20opened%20for%20Presley%20three%20times%20that%20year;%20his%20band's%20style%20shifted%20from%20country%20and%20western%20to%20entirely%20rock%20and%20roll.%20%20In%20October%20that%20year,%20when%20he%20opened%20for%20Bill%20Haley%20&%20His%20Comets,%20he%20was%20spotted%20by%20Nashville%20scout%20Eddie%20Crandall,%20who%20helped%20him%20get%20a%20contract%20with%20Decca%20Records.%20%20Holly's%20recording%20sessions%20at%20Decca%20were%20produced%20by%20Owen%20Bradley.%20%20Unhappy%20with%20Bradley's%20control%20in%20the%20studio%20and%20with%20the%20sound%20he%20achieved%20there,%20he%20went%20to%20producer%20Norman%20Petty%20in%20Clovis,%20New%20Mexico,%20and%20recorded%20a%20demo%20of%20"That'll%20Be%20the%20Day",%20among%20other%20songs.%20%20Petty%20became%20the%20band's%20manager%20and%20sent%20the%20demo%20to%20Brunswick%20Records,%20which%20released%20it%20as%20a%20single%20credited%20to%20"The%20Crickets",%20which%20became%20the%20name%20of%20Holly's%20band.%20%20In%20September%201957,%20as%20the%20band%20toured,%20"That'll%20Be%20the%20Day"%20topped%20the%20US%20"Best%20Sellers%20in%20Stores"%20chart%20and%20the%20UK%20Singles%20Chart.%20%20Its%20success%20was%20followed%20in%20October%20by%20another%20major%20hit,%20"Peggy%20Sue".%20%20The%20album%20Chirping%20Crickets,%20released%20in%20November%201957,%20reached%20number%20five%20on%20the%20UK%20Albums%20Chart.%20%20Holly%20made%20his%20second%20appearance%20on%20The%20Ed%20Sullivan%20Show%20in%20January%201958%20and%20soon%20after,%20toured%20Australia%20and%20then%20the%20UK.%20%20In%20early%201959,%20he%20assembled%20a%20new%20band,%20consisting%20of%20future%20country%20music%20star%20Waylon%20Jennings%20(bass),%20famed%20session%20musician%20Tommy%20Allsup%20(guitar),%20and%20Carl%20Bunch%20(drums),%20and%20embarked%20on%20a%20tour%20of%20the%20midwestern%20U.S.%20%20After%20a%20show%20in%20Clear%20Lake,%20Iowa,%20he%20chartered%20an%20airplane%20to%20travel%20to%20his%20next%20show,%20in%20Moorhead,%20Minnesota.%20%20Soon%20after%20takeoff,%20the%20plane%20crashed,%20killing%20him,%20Ritchie%20Valens,%20The%20Big%20Bopper,%20and%20pilot%20Roger%20Peterson%20in%20a%20tragedy%20later%20referred%20to%20by%20Don%20McLean%20as%20"The%20Day%20the%20Music%20Died".%20%20During%20his%20short%20career,%20Holly%20wrote,%20recorded,%20and%20produced%20his%20own%20material.%20%20He%20is%20often%20regarded%20as%20the%20artist%20who%20defined%20the%20traditional%20rock-and-roll%20lineup%20of%20two%20guitars,%20bass,%20and%20drums.%20%20He%20was%20a%20major%20influence%20on%20later%20popular%20music%20artists,%20including%20Bob%20Dylan,%20The%20Beatles,%20The%20Rolling%20Stones,%20Eric%20Clapton,%20and%20Elton%20John.%20%20He%20was%20among%20the%20first%20artists%20inducted%20into%20the%20Rock%20and%20Roll%20Hall%20of%20Fame,%20in%201986.%20%20Rolling%20Stone%20magazine%20ranked%20him%20number%2013%20in%20its%20list%20of%20"100%20Greatest%20Artists". ,%20"That'll%20Be%20the%20Day"%20topped%20the%20US%20"Best%20Sellers%20in%20Stores"%20chart%20and%20the%20UK%20Singles%20Chart.%20%20Its%20success%20was%20followed%20in%20October%20by%20another%20major%20hit,%20"Peggy%20Sue".%20%20The%20album%20Chirping%20Crickets,%20released%20in%20November%201957,%20reached%20number%20five%20on%20the%20UK%20Albums%20Chart.%20%20Holly%20made%20his%20second%20appearance%20on%20The%20Ed%20Sullivan%20Show%20in%20January%201958%20and%20soon%20after,%20toured%20Australia%20and%20then%20the%20UK.%20%20In%20early%201959,%20he%20assembled%20a%20new%20band,%20consisting%20of%20future%20country%20music%20star%20Waylon%20Jennings%20(bass),%20famed%20session%20musician%20Tommy%20Allsup%20(guitar),%20and%20Carl%20Bunch%20(drums),%20and%20embarked%20on%20a%20tour%20of%20the%20midwestern%20U.S.%20%20After%20a%20show%20in%20Clear%20Lake,%20Iowa,%20he%20chartered%20an%20airplane%20to%20travel%20to%20his%20next%20show,%20in%20Moorhead,%20Minnesota.%20%20Soon%20after%20takeoff,%20the%20plane%20crashed,%20killing%20him,%20Ritchie%20Valens,%20The%20Big%20Bopper,%20and%20pilot%20Roger%20Peterson%20in%20a%20tragedy%20later%20referred%20to%20by%20Don%20McLean%20as%20"The%20Day%20the%20Music%20Died".%20%20During%20his%20short%20career,%20Holly%20wrote,%20recorded,%20and%20produced%20his%20own%20material.%20%20He%20is%20often%20regarded%20as%20the%20artist%20who%20defined%20the%20traditional%20rock-and-roll%20lineup%20of%20two%20guitars,%20bass,%20and%20drums.%20%20He%20was%20a%20major%20influence%20on%20later%20popular%20music%20artists,%20including%20Bob%20Dylan,%20The%20Beatles,%20The%20Rolling%20Stones,%20Eric%20Clapton,%20and%20Elton%20John.%20%20He%20was%20among%20the%20first%20artists%20inducted%20into%20the%20Rock%20and%20Roll%20Hall%20of%20Fame,%20in%201986.%20%20Rolling%20Stone%20magazine%20ranked%20him%20number%2013%20in%20its%20list%20of%20"100%20Greatest%20Artists". Charles%20Hardin%20Holley%20(September%207,%201936%20�%20February%203,%201959),%20known%20as%20Buddy%20Holly,%20was%20an%20American%20musician%20and%20singer-songwriter%20who%20was%20a%20central%20figure%20of%20mid-1950s%20rock%20and%20roll.%20%20He%20was%20born%20in%20Lubbock,%20Texas,%20to%20a%20musical%20family%20during%20the%20Great%20Depression,%20and%20learned%20to%20play%20guitar%20and%20sing%20alongside%20his%20siblings.%20%20His%20style%20was%20influenced%20by%20gospel%20music,%20country%20music,%20and%20rhythm%20and%20blues%20acts,%20and%20he%20performed%20in%20Lubbock%20with%20his%20friends%20from%20high%20school.%20%20He%20made%20his%20first%20appearance%20on%20local%20television%20in%201952,%20and%20the%20following%20year%20he%20formed%20the%20group%20"Buddy%20and%20Bob"%20with%20his%20friend%20Bob%20Montgomery.%20%20In%201955,%20after%20opening%20for%20Elvis%20Presley,%20he%20decided%20to%20pursue%20a%20career%20in%20music.%20%20He%20opened%20for%20Presley%20three%20times%20that%20year;%20his%20band's%20style%20shifted%20from%20country%20and%20western%20to%20entirely%20rock%20and%20roll.%20%20In%20October%20that%20year,%20when%20he%20opened%20for%20Bill%20Haley%20&%20His%20Comets,%20he%20was%20spotted%20by%20Nashville%20scout%20Eddie%20Crandall,%20who%20helped%20him%20get%20a%20contract%20with%20Decca%20Records.%20%20Holly's%20recording%20sessions%20at%20Decca%20were%20produced%20by%20Owen%20Bradley.%20%20Unhappy%20with%20Bradley's%20control%20in%20the%20studio%20and%20with%20the%20sound%20he%20achieved%20there,%20he%20went%20to%20producer%20Norman%20Petty%20in%20Clovis,%20New%20Mexico,%20and%20recorded%20a%20demo%20of%20"That'll%20Be%20the%20Day",%20among%20other%20songs.%20%20Petty%20became%20the%20band's%20manager%20and%20sent%20the%20demo%20to%20Brunswick%20Records,%20which%20released%20it%20as%20a%20single%20credited%20to%20"The%20Crickets",%20which%20became%20the%20name%20of%20Holly's%20band.%20%20In%20September%201957,%20as%20the%20band%20toured,%20"That'll%20Be%20the%20Day"%20topped%20the%20US%20"Best%20Sellers%20in%20Stores"%20chart%20and%20the%20UK%20Singles%20Chart.%20%20Its%20success%20was%20followed%20in%20October%20by%20another%20major%20hit,%20"Peggy%20Sue".%20%20The%20album%20Chirping%20Crickets,%20released%20in%20November%201957,%20reached%20number%20five%20on%20the%20UK%20Albums%20Chart.%20%20Holly%20made%20his%20second%20appearance%20on%20The%20Ed%20Sullivan%20Show%20in%20January%201958%20and%20soon%20after,%20toured%20Australia%20and%20then%20the%20UK.%20%20In%20early%201959,%20he%20assembled%20a%20new%20band,%20consisting%20of%20future%20country%20music%20star%20Waylon%20Jennings%20(bass),%20famed%20session%20musician%20Tommy%20Allsup%20(guitar),%20and%20Carl%20Bunch%20(drums),%20and%20embarked%20on%20a%20tour%20of%20the%20midwestern%20U.S.%20%20After%20a%20show%20in%20Clear%20Lake,%20Iowa,%20he%20chartered%20an%20airplane%20to%20travel%20to%20his%20next%20show,%20in%20Moorhead,%20Minnesota.%20%20Soon%20after%20takeoff,%20the%20plane%20crashed,%20killing%20him,%20Ritchie%20Valens,%20The%20Big%20Bopper,%20and%20pilot%20Roger%20Peterson%20in%20a%20tragedy%20later%20referred%20to%20by%20Don%20McLean%20as%20"The%20Day%20the%20Music%20Died".%20%20During%20his%20short%20career,%20Holly%20wrote,%20recorded,%20and%20produced%20his%20own%20material.%20%20He%20is%20often%20regarded%20as%20the%20artist%20who%20defined%20the%20traditional%20rock-and-roll%20lineup%20of%20two%20guitars,%20bass,%20and%20drums.%20%20He%20was%20a%20major%20influence%20on%20later%20popular%20music%20artists,%20including%20Bob%20Dylan,%20The%20Beatles,%20The%20Rolling%20Stones,%20Eric%20Clapton,%20and%20Elton%20John.%20%20He%20was%20among%20the%20first%20artists%20inducted%20into%20the%20Rock%20and%20Roll%20Hall%20of%20Fame,%20in%201986.%20%20Rolling%20Stone%20magazine%20ranked%20him%20number%2013%20in%20its%20list%20of%20"100%20Greatest%20Artists". Charles%20Hardin%20Holley%20(September%207,%201936%20�%20February%203,%201959),%20known%20as%20Buddy%20Holly,%20was%20an%20American%20musician%20and%20singer-songwriter%20who%20was%20a%20central%20figure%20of%20mid-1950s%20rock%20and%20roll.%20%20He%20was%20born%20in%20Lubbock,%20Texas,%20to%20a%20musical%20family%20during%20the%20Great%20Depression,%20and%20learned%20to%20play%20guitar%20and%20sing%20alongside%20his%20siblings.%20%20His%20style%20was%20influenced%20by%20gospel%20music,%20country%20music,%20and%20rhythm%20and%20blues%20acts,%20and%20he%20performed%20in%20Lubbock%20with%20his%20friends%20from%20high%20school.%20%20He%20made%20his%20first%20appearance%20on%20local%20television%20in%201952,%20and%20the%20following%20year%20he%20formed%20the%20group%20"Buddy%20and%20Bob"%20with%20his%20friend%20Bob%20Montgomery.%20%20In%201955,%20after%20opening%20for%20Elvis%20Presley,%20he%20decided%20to%20pursue%20a%20career%20in%20music.%20%20He%20opened%20for%20Presley%20three%20times%20that%20year;%20his%20band's%20style%20shifted%20from%20country%20and%20western%20to%20entirely%20rock%20and%20roll.%20%20In%20October%20that%20year,%20when%20he%20opened%20for%20Bill%20Haley%20&%20His%20Comets,%20he%20was%20spotted%20by%20Nashville%20scout%20Eddie%20Crandall,%20who%20helped%20him%20get%20a%20contract%20with%20Decca%20Records.%20%20Holly's%20recording%20sessions%20at%20Decca%20were%20produced%20by%20Owen%20Bradley.%20%20Unhappy%20with%20Bradley's%20control%20in%20the%20studio%20and%20with%20the%20sound%20he%20achieved%20there,%20he%20went%20to%20producer%20Norman%20Petty%20in%20Clovis,%20New%20Mexico,%20and%20recorded%20a%20demo%20of%20"That'll%20Be%20the%20Day",%20among%20other%20songs.%20%20Petty%20became%20the%20band's%20manager%20and%20sent%20the%20demo%20to%20Brunswick%20Records,%20which%20released%20it%20as%20a%20single%20credited%20to%20"The%20Crickets",%20which%20became%20the%20name%20of%20Holly's%20band.%20%20In%20September%201957,%20as%20the%20band%20toured,%20"That'll%20Be%20the%20Day"%20topped%20the%20US%20"Best%20Sellers%20in%20Stores"%20chart%20and%20the%20UK%20Singles%20Chart.%20%20Its%20success%20was%20followed%20in%20October%20by%20another%20major%20hit,%20"Peggy%20Sue".%20%20The%20album%20Chirping%20Crickets,%20released%20in%20November%201957,%20reached%20number%20five%20on%20the%20UK%20Albums%20Chart.%20%20Holly%20made%20his%20second%20appearance%20on%20The%20Ed%20Sullivan%20Show%20in%20January%201958%20and%20soon%20after,%20toured%20Australia%20and%20then%20the%20UK.%20%20In%20early%201959,%20he%20assembled%20a%20new%20band,%20consisting%20of%20future%20country%20music%20star%20Waylon%20Jennings%20(bass),%20famed%20session%20musician%20Tommy%20Allsup%20(guitar),%20and%20Carl%20Bunch%20(drums),%20and%20embarked%20on%20a%20tour%20of%20the%20midwestern%20U.S.%20%20After%20a%20show%20in%20Clear%20Lake,%20Iowa,%20he%20chartered%20an%20airplane%20to%20travel%20to%20his%20next%20show,%20in%20Moorhead,%20Minnesota.%20%20Soon%20after%20takeoff,%20the%20plane%20crashed,%20killing%20him,%20Ritchie%20Valens,%20The%20Big%20Bopper,%20and%20pilot%20Roger%20Peterson%20in%20a%20tragedy%20later%20referred%20to%20by%20Don%20McLean%20as%20"The%20Day%20the%20Music%20Died".%20%20During%20his%20short%20career,%20Holly%20wrote,%20recorded,%20and%20produced%20his%20own%20material.%20%20He%20is%20often%20regarded%20as%20the%20artist%20who%20defined%20the%20traditional%20rock-and-roll%20lineup%20of%20two%20guitars,%20bass,%20and%20drums.%20%20He%20was%20a%20major%20influence%20on%20later%20popular%20music%20artists,%20including%20Bob%20Dylan,%20The%20Beatles,%20The%20Rolling%20Stones,%20Eric%20Clapton,%20and%20Elton%20John.%20%20He%20was%20among%20the%20first%20artists%20inducted%20into%20the%20Rock%20and%20Roll%20Hall%20of%20Fame,%20in%201986.%20%20Rolling%20Stone%20magazine%20ranked%20him%20number%2013%20in%20its%20list%20of%20"100%20Greatest%20Artists". The%20Melbourne%20Cricket%20Ground%20(MCG),%20also%20known%20simply%20as%20"The%20G",%20is%20an%20Australian%20sports%20stadium%20located%20in%20Yarra%20Park,%20Melbourne,%20Victoria.%20%20Home%20to%20the%20Melbourne%20Cricket%20Club,%20it%20is%20the%2010th-largest%20stadium%20in%20the%20world,%20the%20largest%20in%20Australia,%20the%20largest%20in%20the%20Southern%20Hemisphere,%20the%20largest%20cricket%20ground%20by%20capacity,%20and%20has%20the%20tallest%20light%20towers%20of%20any%20sporting%20venue.%20%20The%20MCG%20is%20within%20walking%20distance%20of%20the%20city%20centre%20and%20is%20served%20by%20the%20Richmond%20railway%20station,%20Richmond,%20and%20the%20Jolimont%20railway%20station,%20East%20Melbourne.%20%20It%20is%20part%20of%20the%20Melbourne%20Sports%20and%20Entertainment%20Precinct.%20%20Since%20it%20was%20built%20in%201853,%20the%20MCG%20has%20been%20in%20a%20state%20of%20almost%20constant%20renewal.%20%20It%20served%20as%20the%20centrepiece%20stadium%20of%20the%201956%20Summer%20Olympics,%20the%202006%20Commonwealth%20Games%20and%20two%20Cricket%20World%20Cups:%201992%20and%202015.%20%20It%20is%20also%20famous%20for%20its%20role%20in%20the%20development%20of%20international%20cricket;%20it%20was%20the%20venue%20for%20both%20the%20first%20Test%20match%20and%20the%20first%20One%20Day%20International,%20played%20between%20Australia%20and%20England%20in%201877%20and%201971%20respectively.%20%20The%20annual%20Boxing%20Day%20Test%20is%20one%20of%20the%20MCG's%20most%20popular%20events.%20%20Referred%20to%20as%20"the%20spiritual%20home%20of%20Australian%20rules%20football"%20for%20its%20strong%20association%20with%20the%20sport%20since%20it%20was%20codified%20in%201859,%20it%20hosts%20Australian%20Football%20League%20(AFL)%20matches%20in%20the%20winter,%20with%20at%20least%20one%20game%20held%20there%20in%20most%20(if%20not%20all)%20rounds%20of%20the%20premiership%20season.%20%20The%20stadium%20fills%20to%20capacity%20for%20the%20AFL%20Grand%20Final.%20%20Home%20to%20the%20National%20Sports%20Museum,%20the%20MCG%20has%20hosted%20other%20major%20sporting%20events,%20including%20international%20rules%20football%20matches%20between%20Australia%20and%20Ireland,%20international%20rugby%20union%20matches,%20State%20of%20Origin%20(rugby%20league)%20games,%20and%20FIFA%20World%20Cup%20qualifiers.%20%20Concerts%20and%20other%20cultural%20events%20are%20also%20held%20at%20the%20venue,%20with%20the%20record%20attendance%20standing%20at%20around%20130,000%20for%20a%20Billy%20Graham%20evangelistic%20crusade%20in%201959.%20%20Grandstand%20redevelopments%20and%20occupational%20health%20and%20safety%20legislation%20have%20limited%20the%20maximum%20seating%20capacity%20to%20approximately%2095,000%20with%20an%20additional%205,000%20standing%20room%20capacity,%20bringing%20the%20total%20capacity%20to%20100,024.%20%20The%20MCG%20is%20listed%20on%20the%20Victorian%20Heritage%20Register%20and%20was%20included%20on%20the%20Australian%20National%20Heritage%20List%20in%202005.%20%20Journalist%20Greg%20Baum%20called%20it%20"a%20shrine,%20a%20citadel,%20a%20landmark,%20a%20totem"%20that%20"symbolises%20Melbourne%20to%20the%20world". %20Home%20to%20the%20National%20Sports%20Museum,%20the%20MCG%20has%20hosted%20other%20major%20sporting%20events,%20including%20international%20rules%20football%20matches%20between%20Australia%20and%20Ireland,%20international%20rugby%20union%20matches,%20State%20of%20Origin%20(rugby%20league)%20games,%20and%20FIFA%20World%20Cup%20qualifiers.%20%20Concerts%20and%20other%20cultural%20events%20are%20also%20held%20at%20the%20venue,%20with%20the%20record%20attendance%20standing%20at%20around%20130,000%20for%20a%20Billy%20Graham%20evangelistic%20crusade%20in%201959.%20%20Grandstand%20redevelopments%20and%20occupational%20health%20and%20safety%20legislation%20have%20limited%20the%20maximum%20seating%20capacity%20to%20approximately%2095,000%20with%20an%20additional%205,000%20standing%20room%20capacity,%20bringing%20the%20total%20capacity%20to%20100,024.%20%20The%20MCG%20is%20listed%20on%20the%20Victorian%20Heritage%20Register%20and%20was%20included%20on%20the%20Australian%20National%20Heritage%20List%20in%202005.%20%20Journalist%20Greg%20Baum%20called%20it%20"a%20shrine,%20a%20citadel,%20a%20landmark,%20a%20totem"%20that%20"symbolises%20Melbourne%20to%20the%20world". The%20Melbourne%20Cricket%20Ground%20(MCG),%20also%20known%20simply%20as%20"The%20G",%20is%20an%20Australian%20sports%20stadium%20located%20in%20Yarra%20Park,%20Melbourne,%20Victoria.%20%20Home%20to%20the%20Melbourne%20Cricket%20Club,%20it%20is%20the%2010th-largest%20stadium%20in%20the%20world,%20the%20largest%20in%20Australia,%20the%20largest%20in%20the%20Southern%20Hemisphere,%20the%20largest%20cricket%20ground%20by%20capacity,%20and%20has%20the%20tallest%20light%20towers%20of%20any%20sporting%20venue.%20%20The%20MCG%20is%20within%20walking%20distance%20of%20the%20city%20centre%20and%20is%20served%20by%20the%20Richmond%20railway%20station,%20Richmond,%20and%20the%20Jolimont%20railway%20station,%20East%20Melbourne.%20%20It%20is%20part%20of%20the%20Melbourne%20Sports%20and%20Entertainment%20Precinct.%20%20Since%20it%20was%20built%20in%201853,%20the%20MCG%20has%20been%20in%20a%20state%20of%20almost%20constant%20renewal.%20%20It%20served%20as%20the%20centrepiece%20stadium%20of%20the%201956%20Summer%20Olympics,%20the%202006%20Commonwealth%20Games%20and%20two%20Cricket%20World%20Cups:%201992%20and%202015.%20%20It%20is%20also%20famous%20for%20its%20role%20in%20the%20development%20of%20international%20cricket;%20it%20was%20the%20venue%20for%20both%20the%20first%20Test%20match%20and%20the%20first%20One%20Day%20International,%20played%20between%20Australia%20and%20England%20in%201877%20and%201971%20respectively.%20%20The%20annual%20Boxing%20Day%20Test%20is%20one%20of%20the%20MCG's%20most%20popular%20events.%20%20Referred%20to%20as%20"the%20spiritual%20home%20of%20Australian%20rules%20football"%20for%20its%20strong%20association%20with%20the%20sport%20since%20it%20was%20codified%20in%201859,%20it%20hosts%20Australian%20Football%20League%20(AFL)%20matches%20in%20the%20winter,%20with%20at%20least%20one%20game%20held%20there%20in%20most%20(if%20not%20all)%20rounds%20of%20the%20premiership%20season.%20%20The%20stadium%20fills%20to%20capacity%20for%20the%20AFL%20Grand%20Final.%20%20Home%20to%20the%20National%20Sports%20Museum,%20the%20MCG%20has%20hosted%20other%20major%20sporting%20events,%20including%20international%20rules%20football%20matches%20between%20Australia%20and%20Ireland,%20international%20rugby%20union%20matches,%20State%20of%20Origin%20(rugby%20league)%20games,%20and%20FIFA%20World%20Cup%20qualifiers.%20%20Concerts%20and%20other%20cultural%20events%20are%20also%20held%20at%20the%20venue,%20with%20the%20record%20attendance%20standing%20at%20around%20130,000%20for%20a%20Billy%20Graham%20evangelistic%20crusade%20in%201959.%20%20Grandstand%20redevelopments%20and%20occupational%20health%20and%20safety%20legislation%20have%20limited%20the%20maximum%20seating%20capacity%20to%20approximately%2095,000%20with%20an%20additional%205,000%20standing%20room%20capacity,%20bringing%20the%20total%20capacity%20to%20100,024.%20%20The%20MCG%20is%20listed%20on%20the%20Victorian%20Heritage%20Register%20and%20was%20included%20on%20the%20Australian%20National%20Heritage%20List%20in%202005.%20%20Journalist%20Greg%20Baum%20called%20it%20"a%20shrine,%20a%20citadel,%20a%20landmark,%20a%20totem"%20that%20"symbolises%20Melbourne%20to%20the%20world". The%20Melbourne%20Cricket%20Ground%20(MCG),%20also%20known%20simply%20as%20"The%20G",%20is%20an%20Australian%20sports%20stadium%20located%20in%20Yarra%20Park,%20Melbourne,%20Victoria.%20%20Home%20to%20the%20Melbourne%20Cricket%20Club,%20it%20is%20the%2010th-largest%20stadium%20in%20the%20world,%20the%20largest%20in%20Australia,%20the%20largest%20in%20the%20Southern%20Hemisphere,%20the%20largest%20cricket%20ground%20by%20capacity,%20and%20has%20the%20tallest%20light%20towers%20of%20any%20sporting%20venue.%20%20The%20MCG%20is%20within%20walking%20distance%20of%20the%20city%20centre%20and%20is%20served%20by%20the%20Richmond%20railway%20station,%20Richmond,%20and%20the%20Jolimont%20railway%20station,%20East%20Melbourne.%20%20It%20is%20part%20of%20the%20Melbourne%20Sports%20and%20Entertainment%20Precinct.%20%20Since%20it%20was%20built%20in%201853,%20the%20MCG%20has%20been%20in%20a%20state%20of%20almost%20constant%20renewal.%20%20It%20served%20as%20the%20centrepiece%20stadium%20of%20the%201956%20Summer%20Olympics,%20the%202006%20Commonwealth%20Games%20and%20two%20Cricket%20World%20Cups:%201992%20and%202015.%20%20It%20is%20also%20famous%20for%20its%20role%20in%20the%20development%20of%20international%20cricket;%20it%20was%20the%20venue%20for%20both%20the%20first%20Test%20match%20and%20the%20first%20One%20Day%20International,%20played%20between%20Australia%20and%20England%20in%201877%20and%201971%20respectively.%20%20The%20annual%20Boxing%20Day%20Test%20is%20one%20of%20the%20MCG's%20most%20popular%20events.%20%20Referred%20to%20as%20"the%20spiritual%20home%20of%20Australian%20rules%20football"%20for%20its%20strong%20association%20with%20the%20sport%20since%20it%20was%20codified%20in%201859,%20it%20hosts%20Australian%20Football%20League%20(AFL)%20matches%20in%20the%20winter,%20with%20at%20least%20one%20game%20held%20there%20in%20most%20(if%20not%20all)%20rounds%20of%20the%20premiership%20season.%20%20The%20stadium%20fills%20to%20capacity%20for%20the%20AFL%20Grand%20Final.%20%20Home%20to%20the%20National%20Sports%20Museum,%20the%20MCG%20has%20hosted%20other%20major%20sporting%20events,%20including%20international%20rules%20football%20matches%20between%20Australia%20and%20Ireland,%20international%20rugby%20union%20matches,%20State%20of%20Origin%20(rugby%20league)%20games,%20and%20FIFA%20World%20Cup%20qualifiers.%20%20Concerts%20and%20other%20cultural%20events%20are%20also%20held%20at%20the%20venue,%20with%20the%20record%20attendance%20standing%20at%20around%20130,000%20for%20a%20Billy%20Graham%20evangelistic%20crusade%20in%201959.%20%20Grandstand%20redevelopments%20and%20occupational%20health%20and%20safety%20legislation%20have%20limited%20the%20maximum%20seating%20capacity%20to%20approximately%2095,000%20with%20an%20additional%205,000%20standing%20room%20capacity,%20bringing%20the%20total%20capacity%20to%20100,024.%20%20The%20MCG%20is%20listed%20on%20the%20Victorian%20Heritage%20Register%20and%20was%20included%20on%20the%20Australian%20National%20Heritage%20List%20in%202005.%20%20Journalist%20Greg%20Baum%20called%20it%20"a%20shrine,%20a%20citadel,%20a%20landmark,%20a%20totem"%20that%20"symbolises%20Melbourne%20to%20the%20world". e%20umpire%20at%20the%20bowler's%20end%20considers%20that%20by%20their%20repetition%20and%20taking%20into%20account%20their%20length,%20height%20and%20direction%20they%20are%20likely%20to%20inflict%20physical%20injury%20on%20the%20striker".%20%20The%20occasional%20short-pitched%20ball%20aimed%20at%20the%20batsman%20(a%20bouncer)%20has%20never%20been%20illegal%20and%20is%20still%20in%20widespread%20use%20as%20a%20tactic. The%20flipper%20is%20the%20name%20of%20a%20particular%20bowling%20delivery%20used%20in%20cricket,%20generally%20by%20a%20leg%20spin%20bowler.%20%20In%20essence%20it%20is%20a%20back%20spin%20ball.%20%20Squeezed%20out%20of%20the%20front%20of%20the%20hand%20with%20the%20thumb%20and%20first%20and%20second%20fingers,%20it%20keeps%20deceptively%20low%20after%20pitching%20and%20can%20accordingly%20be%20very%20difficult%20to%20play.%20%20The%20flipper%20is%20comparable%20to%20a%20riseball%20in%20fast-pitch%20softball.%20%20%20By%20putting%20backspin%20on%20the%20ball%20the%20Magnus%20effect%20results%20in%20air%20travelling%20over%20the%20top%20of%20the%20ball%20quickly%20and%20cleanly%20whilst%20air%20travelling%20under%20the%20ball%20is%20turbulent.%20%20The%20lift%20produced%20means%20that%20the%20ball%20drops%20slower%20and%20travels%20further%20than%20a%20normal%20delivery.%20%20The%20slower%20descent%20also%20results%20in%20the%20ball%20bouncing%20lower.%20%20The%20flipper%20is%20bowled%20on%20the%20opposite%20side%20to%20a%20slider,%20much%20in%20the%20same%20way%20that%20the%20top-spinner%20is%20bowled.%20%20On%20release,%20the%20bowler%20'pinches'%20or%20clicks%20the%20thumb%20and%20forefinger,%20causing%20the%20ball%20to%20come%20out%20underneath%20the%20hand.%20%20There%20must%20be%20sufficient%20tension%20in%20the%20wrist%20and%20fingers%20to%20impart%20a%20good%20helping%20of%20backspin%20or%20underspin.%20%20In%20doing%20so%20the%20flipper%20will%20float%20on%20towards%20the%20batsman%20and%20land%20on%20a%20fuller%20length%20than%20he%20anticipated,%20often%20leaving%20him%20caught%20on%20the%20back%20foot%20when%20he%20wrongly%20assumes%20it%20to%20be%20a%20pullable%20or%20a%20cuttable%20ball.%20%20The%20back%20spin%20or%20underspin%20will%20cause%20the%20ball%20to%20hurry%20on%20at%20great%20pace%20with%20very%20little%20bounce,%20though%20this%20may%20be%20harder%20to%20achieve%20on%20softer%20wickets.%20%20A%20series%20of%20normal%20leg%20spinners%20or%20 The%20flipper%20is%20the%20name%20of%20a%20particular%20bowling%20delivery%20used%20in%20cricket,%20generally%20by%20a%20leg%20spin%20bowler.%20%20In%20essence%20it%20is%20a%20back%20spin%20ball.%20%20Squeezed%20out%20of%20the%20front%20of%20the%20hand%20with%20the%20thumb%20and%20first%20and%20second%20fingers,%20it%20keeps%20deceptively%20low%20after%20pitching%20and%20can%20accordingly%20be%20very%20difficult%20to%20play.%20%20The%20flipper%20is%20comparable%20to%20a%20riseball%20in%20fast-pitch%20softball.%20%20%20By%20putting%20backspin%20on%20the%20ball%20the%20Magnus%20effect%20results%20in%20air%20travelling%20over%20the%20top%20of%20the%20ball%20quickly%20and%20cleanly%20whilst%20air%20travelling%20under%20the%20ball%20is%20turbulent.%20%20The%20lift%20produced%20means%20that%20the%20ball%20drops%20slower%20and%20travels%20further%20than%20a%20normal%20delivery.%20%20The%20slower%20descent%20also%20results%20in%20the%20ball%20bouncing%20lower.%20%20The%20flipper%20is%20bowled%20on%20the%20opposite%20side%20to%20a%20slider,%20much%20in%20the%20same%20way%20that%20the%20top-spinner%20is%20bowled.%20%20On%20release,%20the%20bowler%20'pinches'%20or%20clicks%20the%20thumb%20and%20forefinger,%20causing%20the%20ball%20to%20come%20out%20underneath%20the%20hand.%20%20There%20must%20be%20sufficient%20tension%20in%20the%20wrist%20and%20fingers%20to%20impart%20a%20good%20helping%20of%20backspin%20or%20underspin.%20%20In%20doing%20so%20the%20flipper%20will%20float%20on%20towards%20the%20batsman%20and%20land%20on%20a%20fuller%20length%20than%20he%20anticipated,%20often%20leaving%20him%20caught%20on%20the%20back%20foot%20when%20he%20wrongly%20assumes%20it%20to%20be%20a%20pullable%20or%20a%20cuttable%20ball.%20%20The%20back%20spin%20or%20underspin%20will%20cause%20the%20ball%20to%20hurry%20on%20at%20great%20pace%20with%20very%20little%20bounce,%20though%20this%20may%20be%20harder%20to%20achieve%20on%20softer%20wickets.%20%20A%20series%20of%20normal%20leg%20spinners%20or%20
